> **RENDER PARITY LAW (2026-07-07, Yair): the onboarding flow has ONE source of truth = the render (gg-onboarding-render.pages.dev). A required `render_parity` CI job fetches the render's OWN published export (live JSON, NOT a committed snapshot) and asserts the built flow order + copy match it, AND a full onboarding parity walk (behavior) gates EVERY build. No merge, no promote unless both pass. Primary conductor gate, alongside the evidence gate. Report-mode until main first matches the render, then flips to required. Detail in CONDUCTOR-RUNS-LEAN.md section 0.**
> **REGRESSION RULE (2026-07-07, Yair): every acceptance verdict and every round judge names regressions EXPLICITLY (worked-before / broke-now / introduced-by-which-change) and logs them to `docs/fix-reports/REGRESSIONS.md`. A regression's fix always links back to the change that caused it, never fixed out of context.**
> **GITLAB HOME: gitlab.guidedgrowthapp.com (migrated 2026-07-04; gitlab.com archived/read-only — do not push there).**
> **TRUNK CUTOVER 2026-07-04 (~16:00): the `staging` branch was merged into `main` and DELETED.**
> `main` is now the only trunk. Everywhere the plans and standing rules say "branch off / merge to
> CURRENT origin/staging", read **origin/main**. Open MRs were retargeted (!425 !426 by the conductor;
> !411 !415 auto). The CI gg-qa-iota alias rule was fixed to key on main (!429). No production deploy
> occurred: this CI has no prod job; Yair to confirm the Vercel project's production-branch setting.

Onboarding beat openers were NEVER wired to real per-word timestamps: speakOpener.ts computes reveal from audio.currentTime/audio.duration (start/end anchored, drifts mid-line) and falls to a flat ~310ms/word timer when Chrome reports duration=Infinity (common for streamed MP3). openerReveal.ts does Math.round(progress*wordCount), linear interpolation, not word boundaries. The REAL machinery EXISTS and works but only on the post-onboarding CHECK-IN CHAT: api/cartesia-tts-sse.ts requests add_timestamps:true and src/lib/services/cartesiaVoice.ts schedules real per-word onsets; onboarding uses the plain api/cartesia-tts.ts (MP3 blob, no timestamps). A 2026-06-25 commit downgraded the live DIALOGUE-turn reveal word->sentence when TTS moved ws->http; a 2026-07-02 commit rebuilt real word-sync via SSE but scoped to check-in only. The opener path predates all that (never timestamp-wired). FIX (clean reuse, not rebuild): point useBeatOpenerCartesia/speakOpener at cartesia-tts-sse (add_timestamps) and reuse cartesiaVoice.ts word-onset scheduling instead of openerReveal's progress*wordCount.
